🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\util.ts", "content": "/** Small, dependency-free helpers shared across the server. */\n\n/**\n * Sanitize an arbitrary string into a Slack-safe slug: lowercase, only\n * [a-z0-9-_], collapsed and trimmed dashes. Slack channel names are limited to\n * lowercase letters, numbers, hyphens and underscores (\u2264 80 chars total).\n */\nexport function slugify(input: string): string {\n return input\n .toLowerCase()\n .trim()\n .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-')\n .replace(/^-+|-+$/g, '')\n .replace(/-{2,}/g, '-');\n}\n\n/** Derive a slug from an email's local part (before the @). */\nexport function emailSlug(email: string): string {\n const local = email.split('@')[0] ?? email;\n return slugify(local);\n}\n\n/**\n * Build a Slack channel name `txn-<consultant>-<client>-<seq>` clamped to Slack's\n * 80-char limit. The sequence segment is preserved; the party slugs are trimmed\n * proportionally if the combined name would exceed the limit.\n */\nexport function buildChannelName(consultantSlug: string, clientSlug: string, seq: number): string {\n const prefix = 'txn-';\n const suffix = `-${seq}`;\n const budget = 80 - prefix.length - suffix.length - 1; // 1 for the dash between parties\n let c = consultantSlug;\n let k = clientSlug;\n if (c.length + k.length > budget) {\n const half = Math.floor(budget / 2);\n c = c.slice(0, half);\n k = k.slice(0, budget - c.length);\n }\n return `${prefix}${c}-${k}${suffix}`.replace(/-{2,}/g, '-').slice(0, 80);\n}\n\n/** Stable key for the (consultant, client) pair used for channel reuse. */\nexport function pairKey(consultantId: string, clientEmail: string): string {\n return `${consultantId}::${clientEmail.trim().toLowerCase()}`;\n}\n\n/** Convert a possibly-bigint cents value to a finite number, or null. */\nexport function centsToNumber(value: bigint | number | null | undefined): number | null {\n if (value == null) return null;\n return typeof value === 'bigint' ? Number(value) : value;\n}\n\n/** Format integer cents as a currency string, e.g. 9900 -> \"$99.00\". */\nexport function formatCents(cents: number | null, currency = 'USD'): string {\n if (cents == null) return 'n/a';\n const symbol = currency === 'USD' ? '$' : '';\n return `${symbol}${(cents / 100).toFixed(2)}`;\n}\n" }

🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\stores\\sessionStore.ts", "content": "import { randomUUID } from 'node:crypto';\nimport { config } from '../config.js';\nimport type { SessionData } from '../types.js';\n\n/**\n * Live, in-memory session store (plan \u00a74.3). Holds the current submission, the\n * last result, and a per-session idempotency cache so multi-step flows work\n * without re-sending everything. A TTL sweep clears idle sessions so memory does\n * not grow unbounded. DB-ready: the get/put/delete/sweep surface is the only\n * thing routes depend on \u2014 swapping to Redis/Postgres is a per-file change.\n */\nclass SessionStore {\n private readonly sessions = new Map<string, SessionData>();\n private readonly ttlMs = config.SESSION_TTL_MINUTES * 60_000;\n private sweepTimer: NodeJS.Timeout | null = null;\n\n /** Returns a live session, or null if absent/expired. Touches on read. */\n get(sessionId: string): SessionData | null {\n const s = this.sessions.get(sessionId);\n if (!s) return null;\n if (this.isExpired(s)) {\n this.sessions.delete(sessionId);\n return null;\n }\n s.updatedAt = Date.now();\n return s;\n }\n\n /** Get the session for an id, creating it if missing (used at flow entry). */\n ensure(sessionId?: string): SessionData {\n const id = sessionId && sessionId.trim() ? sessionId.trim() : randomUUID();\n const existing = this.get(id);\n if (existing) return existing;\n const now = Date.now();\n const fresh: SessionData = {\n sessionId: id,\n lastSubmission: null,\n lastResult: null,\n idempotency: {},\n createdAt: now,\n updatedAt: now,\n };\n this.sessions.set(id, fresh);\n return fresh;\n }\n\n put(session: SessionData): void {\n session.updatedAt = Date.now();\n this.sessions.set(session.sessionId, session);\n }\n\n delete(sessionId: string): void {\n this.sessions.delete(sessionId);\n }\n\n size(): number {\n return this.sessions.size;\n }\n\n /** Remove all expired sessions; returns the number swept. */\n sweep(): number {\n let removed = 0;\n for (const [id, s] of this.sessions) {\n if (this.isExpired(s)) {\n this.sessions.delete(id);\n removed += 1;\n }\n }\n return removed;\n }\n\n /** Start the periodic sweep. Unref'd so it never keeps the process alive. */\n startSweeper(): void {\n if (this.sweepTimer) return;\n this.sweepTimer = setInterval(() => this.sweep(), this.ttlMs).unref();\n }\n\n stopSweeper(): void {\n if (this.sweepTimer) {\n clearInterval(this.sweepTimer);\n this.sweepTimer = null;\n }\n }\n\n private isExpired(s: SessionData): boolean {\n return Date.now() - s.updatedAt > this.ttlMs;\n }\n}\n\nexport const sessionStore = new SessionStore();\n" }

🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\stores\\transactionStore.ts", "content": "import { randomUUID } from 'node:crypto';\nimport { pairKey } from '../util.js';\nimport type { ChannelInfo, TransactionRecord, TransactionType } from '../types.js';\n\n/**\n * Live, in-memory transaction store (plan \u00a74.3). Holds transaction state plus\n * the `(consultant, client) \u2192 channel` map that powers channel reuse: the first\n * action for a pair creates the private channel; later actions reuse it.\n * DB-ready behind a small get/put/update surface.\n */\nclass TransactionStore {\n private readonly txns = new Map<string, TransactionRecord>();\n private readonly channelByPair = new Map<string, ChannelInfo>();\n private seq = 0;\n\n /** Monotonic sequence used to keep generated channel names unique. */\n nextSeq(): number {\n this.seq += 1;\n return this.seq;\n }\n\n create(input: {\n consultantId: string;\n clientEmail: string;\n type: TransactionType;\n }): TransactionRecord {\n const now = Date.now();\n const txn: TransactionRecord = {\n txnId: randomUUID(),\n consultantId: input.consultantId,\n clientEmail: input.clientEmail.trim().toLowerCase(),\n type: input.type,\n state: 'started',\n channelId: null,\n channelName: null,\n subscriptionId: null,\n customerId: null,\n lastError: null,\n createdAt: now,\n updatedAt: now,\n };\n this.txns.set(txn.txnId, txn);\n return txn;\n }\n\n get(txnId: string): TransactionRecord | null {\n return this.txns.get(txnId) ?? null;\n }\n\n update(txnId: string, patch: Partial<TransactionRecord>): TransactionRecord | null {\n const txn = this.txns.get(txnId);\n if (!txn) return null;\n Object.assign(txn, patch, { updatedAt: Date.now() });\n return txn;\n }\n\n /** Look up the existing channel for a pair, or null. */\n getChannelForPair(consultantId: string, clientEmail: string): ChannelInfo | null {\n return this.channelByPair.get(pairKey(consultantId, clientEmail)) ?? null;\n }\n\n /** Bind a channel to a pair so subsequent actions reuse it. */\n setChannelForPair(consultantId: string, clientEmail: string, channel: ChannelInfo): void {\n this.channelByPair.set(pairKey(consultantId, clientEmail), channel);\n }\n\n list(): TransactionRecord[] {\n return [...this.txns.values()];\n }\n\n size(): number {\n return this.txns.size;\n }\n}\n\nexport const transactionStore = new TransactionStore();\n" }

🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\services\\maxioService.ts", "content": "import { ApiError, CollectionMethod } from '@maxio-com/advanced-billing-sdk';\nimport { getMaxioClient } from '../maxioClient.js';\nimport { centsToNumber } from '../util.js';\nimport type { CollectionMethodInput, SubscriptionResult } from '../types.js';\n\n/**\n * Typed error thrown by maxioService. Carries an HTTP-ish status code and a\n * human-readable summary so routes can translate it into the `maxio_failed`\n * response shape and post a failure block to Slack.\n */\nexport class MaxioServiceError extends Error {\n readonly statusCode: number;\n constructor(message: string, statusCode = 502) {\n super(message);\n this.name = 'MaxioServiceError';\n this.statusCode = statusCode;\n }\n}\n\n/** Normalize any thrown value (ApiError or otherwise) into a MaxioServiceError. */\nfunction toServiceError(err: unknown, context: string): MaxioServiceError {\n if (err instanceof ApiError) {\n const result = err.result as { errors?: unknown; error?: unknown } | undefined;\n let detail: string | undefined;\n if (result && Array.isArray(result.errors)) {\n detail = result.errors.map((e) => String(e)).join('; ');\n } else if (result && typeof result.error === 'string') {\n detail = result.error;\n } else if (typeof err.body === 'string' && err.body.trim()) {\n detail = err.body.trim();\n }\n const message = detail\n ? `${context}: ${detail} (HTTP ${err.statusCode})`\n : `${context}: Maxio request failed (HTTP ${err.statusCode})`;\n return new MaxioServiceError(message, err.statusCode);\n }\n if (err instanceof Error) {\n return new MaxioServiceError(`${context}: ${err.message}`);\n }\n return new MaxioServiceError(`${context}: ${String(err)}`);\n}\n\nconst COLLECTION_METHOD: Record<CollectionMethodInput, CollectionMethod> = {\n automatic: CollectionMethod.Automatic,\n remittance: CollectionMethod.Remittance,\n};\n\nexport interface CreateSubscriptionInput {\n productHandle: string;\n firstName: string;\n lastName: string;\n email: string;\n collectionMethod: CollectionMethodInput;\n couponCode?: string | undefined;\n}\n\n/**\n * UC1 \u2014 create a subscription. The customer is created inline from the submitted\n * name/email; the email doubles as the customer `reference`, so Maxio reuses an\n * existing customer on a retried submission (idempotent customer). The payment\n * collection method and optional coupon are passed through. Returns plan, MRR,\n * state and the next assessment date read back from the created subscription.\n */\nexport async function createSubscription(\n input: CreateSubscriptionInput,\n): Promise<SubscriptionResult> {\n const client = getMaxioClient();\n try {\n const { result } = await client.subscriptionsController.createSubscription({\n subscription: {\n productHandle: input.productHandle,\n customerAttributes: {\n firstName: input.firstName,\n lastName: input.lastName,\n email: input.email,\n reference: input.email.trim().toLowerCase(),\n },\n paymentCollectionMethod: COLLECTION_METHOD[input.collectionMethod],\n ...(input.couponCode ? { couponCode: input.couponCode } : {}),\n },\n });\n\n const sub = result.subscription;\n if (!sub || sub.id == null) {\n throw new MaxioServiceError('UC1 createSubscription: Maxio returned no subscription', 502);\n }\n\n const mrr =\n centsToNumber(sub.productPriceInCents) ?? centsToNumber(sub.product?.priceInCents) ?? 0;\n\n return {\n subscriptionId: sub.id,\n customerId: sub.customer?.id ?? null,\n state: sub.state ? String(sub.state) : 'unknown',\n productHandle: sub.product?.handle ?? input.productHandle,\n productName: sub.product?.name ?? input.productHandle,\n mrrInCents: mrr,\n currency: 'USD',\n nextAssessmentAt: sub.nextAssessmentAt ?? null,\n currentPeriodEndsAt: sub.currentPeriodEndsAt ?? null,\n couponCode: input.couponCode ?? null,\n };\n } catch (err) {\n if (err instanceof MaxioServiceError) throw err;\n throw toServiceError(err, 'UC1 createSubscription');\n }\n}\n" }

🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\services\\slackService.ts", "content": "import { WebClient } from '@slack/web-api';\nimport type { KnownBlock } from '@slack/web-api';\nimport { config } from '../config.js';\nimport { formatCents } from '../util.js';\nimport type { ChannelInfo, SubscriptionResult } from '../types.js';\n\n/**\n * Slack Web API integration (plan \u00a73). Uses bot-token capabilities only:\n * users.lookupByEmail (users:read.email) \u2014 resolve party \u2192 user id\n * conversations.create (groups:write) \u2014 create the private channel\n * conversations.list (groups:read) \u2014 reuse on name_taken\n * conversations.invite (groups:write) \u2014 invite workspace members\n * chat.postMessage (chat:write) \u2014 narrate the transaction\n * auth.test \u2014 boot health check\n *\n * Principle: Slack is notification, never the source of truth. Channel/invite/\n * message failures are caught and logged; they never throw into a route.\n */\n\nlet web: WebClient | null = null;\n\nfunction getWeb(): WebClient {\n if (!web) {\n if (!config.SLACK_BOT_TOKEN) {\n throw new Error('SLACK_BOT_TOKEN is not set.');\n }\n web = new WebClient(config.SLACK_BOT_TOKEN);\n }\n return web;\n}\n\n/** Extract a Slack API error code (e.g. \"users_not_found\") from a thrown error. */\nfunction slackErrorCode(err: unknown): string | null {\n if (err && typeof err === 'object' && 'data' in err) {\n const data = (err as { data?: { error?: unknown } }).data;\n if (data && typeof data.error === 'string') return data.error;\n }\n return null;\n}\n\nexport interface SlackAuthStatus {\n ok: boolean;\n error?: string;\n}\n\n/** Boot health check \u2014 confirms the bot token works (plan \u00a73.1). */\nexport async function verifyAuth(): Promise<SlackAuthStatus> {\n if (!config.SLACK_BOT_TOKEN) return { ok: false, error: 'no_token' };\n try {\n const res = await getWeb().auth.test();\n return { ok: Boolean(res.ok) };\n } catch (err) {\n return { ok: false, error: slackErrorCode(err) ?? 'auth_failed' };\n }\n}\n\n/** Resolve an email to a workspace user id, or null if not a member. */\nexport async function lookupUserByEmail(email: string): Promise<string | null> {\n try {\n const res = await getWeb().users.lookupByEmail({ email });\n return res.user?.id ?? null;\n } catch (err) {\n const code = slackErrorCode(err);\n if (code === 'users_not_found') return null;\n console.warn(`[slack] users.lookupByEmail(${email}) failed: ${code ?? String(err)}`);\n return null;\n }\n}\n\n/** Find an existing private channel by exact name (used on name_taken). */\nasync function findChannelByName(name: string): Promise<ChannelInfo | null> {\n try {\n let cursor: string | undefined;\n do {\n const res = await getWeb().conversations.list({\n types: 'private_channel',\n exclude_archived: true,\n limit: 200,\n ...(cursor ? { cursor } : {}),\n });\n const match = res.channels?.find((c) => c.name === name);\n if (match?.id) return { id: match.id, name: match.name ?? name };\n cursor = res.response_metadata?.next_cursor || undefined;\n } while (cursor);\n } catch (err) {\n console.warn(`[slack] conversations.list failed: ${slackErrorCode(err) ?? String(err)}`);\n }\n return null;\n}\n\n/** Invite a single user; treats \"already in channel\" as success. */\nasync function inviteUser(channelId: string, userId: string): Promise<boolean> {\n try {\n await getWeb().conversations.invite({ channel: channelId, users: userId });\n return true;\n } catch (err) {\n const code = slackErrorCode(err);\n if (code === 'already_in_channel') return true;\n console.warn(`[slack] conversations.invite(${channelId}, ${userId}) failed: ${code ?? String(err)}`);\n return false;\n }\n}\n\nexport interface EnsureChannelParams {\n consultantSlug: string;\n consultantSlackEmail: string | null;\n clientEmail: string;\n clientSlug: string;\n channelSeq: number;\n /** Existing channel for this pair, if any \u2014 reused without re-inviting. */\n existing: ChannelInfo | null;\n}\n\nexport interface EnsureChannelResult {\n channel: ChannelInfo | null;\n reused: boolean;\n consultantInvited: boolean;\n clientInvited: boolean;\n clientNotifiedByEmail: boolean;\n notes: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Create (or reuse) the private channel for a (consultant, client) pair and\n * invite both parties using the two-tier strategy (plan \u00a73.2): a party that is a\n * workspace member is invited directly; a party that cannot be added falls back\n * to email-only notification. Never throws \u2014 billing must proceed regardless.\n */\nexport async function ensureTxnChannel(\n params: EnsureChannelParams,\n): Promise<EnsureChannelResult> {\n const notes: string[] = [];\n\n // Reuse path: a channel already exists for this pair.\n if (params.existing) {\n return {\n channel: params.existing,\n reused: true,\n consultantInvited: true,\n clientInvited: true,\n clientNotifiedByEmail: false,\n notes: ['Reused existing transaction channel.'],\n };\n }\n\n const name = `txn-${params.consultantSlug}-${params.clientSlug}-${params.channelSeq}`\n .replace(/-{2,}/g, '-')\n .slice(0, 80);\n\n let channel: ChannelInfo | null = null;\n try {\n const res = await getWeb().conversations.create({ name, is_private: true });\n if (res.channel?.id) {\n channel = { id: res.channel.id, name: res.channel.name ?? name };\n }\n } catch (err) {\n const code = slackErrorCode(err);\n if (code === 'name_taken') {\n channel = await findChannelByName(name);\n if (channel) notes.push('Channel name already existed \u2014 reused it.');\n }\n if (!channel) {\n console.warn(`[slack] conversations.create(${name}) failed: ${code ?? String(err)}`);\n notes.push(`Channel could not be created (${code ?? 'error'}); updates not posted to Slack.`);\n }\n }\n\n let consultantInvited = false;\n let clientInvited = false;\n let clientNotifiedByEmail = false;\n\n if (channel) {\n // Tier 1 \u2014 consultant (if a workspace email is configured).\n if (params.consultantSlackEmail) {\n const consultantId = await lookupUserByEmail(params.consultantSlackEmail);\n if (consultantId) {\n consultantInvited = await inviteUser(channel.id, consultantId);\n }\n if (!consultantInvited) notes.push('Consultant not invited (not a workspace member).');\n } else {\n notes.push('No consultant Slack email configured \u2014 consultant not invited.');\n }\n\n // Tier 1 \u2192 Tier 2 \u2014 client.\n const clientId = await lookupUserByEmail(params.clientEmail);\n if (clientId) {\n clientInvited = await inviteUser(channel.id, clientId);\n }\n if (!clientInvited) {\n clientNotifiedByEmail = true;\n notes.push('Client not a workspace member \u2014 notified by email instead.');\n }\n }\n\n return { channel, reused: false, consultantInvited, clientInvited, clientNotifiedByEmail, notes };\n}\n\n/** Post a message; never throws (failure isolation). Returns success. */\nexport async function postMessage(\n channelId: string | null,\n text: string,\n blocks: KnownBlock[],\n): Promise<boolean> {\n if (!channelId) return false;\n try {\n await getWeb().chat.postMessage({ channel: channelId, text, blocks });\n return true;\n } catch (err) {\n console.warn(`[slack] chat.postMessage(${channelId}) failed: ${slackErrorCode(err) ?? String(err)}`);\n return false;\n }\n}\n\n// --- Pure Block Kit builders (plan \u00a75) \u2014 unit-testable without touching Slack ---\n\nexport function buildTxnStartedBlocks(input: {\n consultantName: string;\n clientEmail: string;\n type: string;\n}): KnownBlock[] {\n return [\n { type: 'header', text: { type: 'plain_text', text: ':wave: Transaction started', emoji: true } },\n {\n type: 'section',\n fields: [\n { type: 'mrkdwn', text: `*Consultant:*\\n${input.consultantName}` },\n { type: 'mrkdwn', text: `*Client:*\\n${input.clientEmail}` },\n { type: 'mrkdwn', text: `*Type:*\\n${input.type}` },\n ],\n },\n ];\n}\n\nexport function buildBookingStartedBlocks(productHandle: string): KnownBlock[] {\n return [\n {\n type: 'section',\n text: {\n type: 'mrkdwn',\n text: `:hourglass_flowing_sand: *Booking started* \u2014 creating your subscription on *${productHandle}*\u2026`,\n },\n },\n ];\n}\n\nexport function buildSubscriptionActiveBlocks(input: {\n result: SubscriptionResult;\n customerName: string;\n maxioUrl: string;\n}): KnownBlock[] {\n const { result } = input;\n const fields: { type: 'mrkdwn'; text: string }[] = [\n { type: 'mrkdwn', text: `*Customer:*\\n${input.customerName}` },\n { type: 'mrkdwn', text: `*Plan:*\\n${result.productName} (\\`${result.productHandle}\\`)` },\n { type: 'mrkdwn', text: `*MRR:*\\n${formatCents(result.mrrInCents, result.currency)} / month` },\n { type: 'mrkdwn', text: `*State:*\\n${result.state}` },\n ];\n if (result.nextAssessmentAt) {\n fields.push({ type: 'mrkdwn', text: `*Next bill:*\\n${result.nextAssessmentAt}` });\n }\n return [\n { type: 'header', text: { type: 'plain_text', text: ':tada: Subscription active', emoji: true } },\n { type: 'section', fields },\n {\n type: 'actions',\n elements: [\n {\n type: 'button',\n text: { type: 'plain_text', text: 'View in Maxio', emoji: true },\n url: input.maxioUrl,\n action_id: 'view_in_maxio',\n },\n ],\n },\n ];\n}\n\nexport function buildFailureBlocks(useCase: string, error: string): KnownBlock[] {\n return [\n { type: 'header', text: { type: 'plain_text', text: `:warning: ${useCase} failed`, emoji: true } },\n { type: 'section', text: { type: 'mrkdwn', text: `*Error:*\\n${error}` } },\n ];\n}\n\nexport function buildEmailFallbackNoteBlocks(): KnownBlock[] {\n return [\n {\n type: 'context',\n elements: [\n {\n type: 'mrkdwn',\n text: ':email: The client is not a workspace member and will be notified by email.',\n },\n ],\n },\n ];\n}\n" }

🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\routes\\book.ts", "content": "import { Router, type Request, type Response } from 'express';\nimport { createHash } from 'node:crypto';\nimport { bookSchema } from '../schemas/book.js';\nimport { findConsultant } from '../constants.js';\nimport { sessionStore } from '../stores/sessionStore.js';\nimport { transactionStore } from '../stores/transactionStore.js';\nimport { createSubscription, MaxioServiceError } from '../services/maxioService.js';\nimport { maxioSubscriptionUrl } from '../maxioClient.js';\nimport {\n ensureTxnChannel,\n postMessage,\n buildTxnStartedBlocks,\n buildBookingStartedBlocks,\n buildSubscriptionActiveBlocks,\n buildFailureBlocks,\n buildEmailFallbackNoteBlocks,\n} from '../services/slackService.js';\nimport { emailSlug } from '../util.js';\nimport type { SubscriptionResult } from '../types.js';\n\nexport const bookRouter = Router();\n\n/**\n * UC1 \u2014 Book & Subscribe. Core loop (plan \u00a71.5): validate \u2192 store \u2192 ensure the\n * transaction's private channel \u2192 post \"started\" \u2192 drive the Maxio subscription\n * \u2192 post completion/failure. Slack failures never block the HTTP response\n * (plan \u00a76); the billing result is the source of truth.\n */\nbookRouter.post('/book', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n // 1. Validate (AC-18) \u2014 no external calls before this passes.\n const parsed = bookSchema.safeParse(req.body);\n if (!parsed.success) {\n return res.status(400).json({\n status: 'invalid',\n errors: parsed.error.issues.map((i) => ({ path: i.path.join('.'), message: i.message })),\n });\n }\n const input = parsed.data;\n\n // 2. Resolve consultant (seeded label on the transaction).\n const consultant = findConsultant(input.consultantId);\n if (!consultant) {\n return res.status(400).json({\n status: 'invalid',\n errors: [{ path: 'consultantId', message: `unknown consultant '${input.consultantId}'` }],\n });\n }\n\n const session = sessionStore.ensure(input.sessionId);\n\n // 3. Session-scoped idempotency (AC-07): an identical resubmission within the\n // same session returns the cached result instead of creating a duplicate.\n const idemKey = createHash('sha256')\n .update([input.email, input.consultantId, input.productHandle, input.collectionMethod].join('|'))\n .digest('hex');\n const cached = session.idempotency[idemKey] as\n | { txnId: string; channelId: string | null; channelName: string | null; subscription: SubscriptionResult }\n | undefined;\n if (cached) {\n return res.json({ status: 'ok', idempotent: true, ...cached });\n }\n\n // 4. Create the transaction record and store the submission.\n const txn = transactionStore.create({\n consultantId: consultant.id,\n clientEmail: input.email,\n type: 'subscription',\n });\n session.lastSubmission = input;\n sessionStore.put(session);\n\n // 5. Ensure the private channel (reuse if the pair already has one).\n const existing = transactionStore.getChannelForPair(consultant.id, input.email);\n const channelResult = await ensureTxnChannel({\n consultantSlug: consultant.slug,\n consultantSlackEmail: consultant.slackEmail,\n clientEmail: input.email,\n clientSlug: emailSlug(input.email),\n channelSeq: transactionStore.nextSeq(),\n existing,\n });\n if (channelResult.channel) {\n transactionStore.update(txn.txnId, {\n channelId: channelResult.channel.id,\n channelName: channelResult.channel.name,\n });\n if (!existing) {\n transactionStore.setChannelForPair(consultant.id, input.email, channelResult.channel);\n }\n }\n const channelId = channelResult.channel?.id ?? null;\n\n // 6. Post \"started\" messages (best-effort).\n if (!channelResult.reused) {\n await postMessage(\n channelId,\n 'Transaction started',\n buildTxnStartedBlocks({\n consultantName: consultant.name,\n clientEmail: input.email,\n type: 'Book & Subscribe',\n }),\n );\n if (channelResult.clientNotifiedByEmail) {\n await postMessage(channelId, 'Client notified by email', buildEmailFallbackNoteBlocks());\n }\n }\n await postMessage(channelId, 'Booking started', buildBookingStartedBlocks(input.productHandle));\n\n // 7. Drive the Maxio subscription.\n try {\n const result = await createSubscription({\n productHandle: input.productHandle,\n firstName: input.firstName,\n lastName: input.lastName,\n email: input.email,\n collectionMethod: input.collectionMethod,\n couponCode: input.couponCode,\n });\n\n transactionStore.update(txn.txnId, {\n state: 'completed',\n subscriptionId: result.subscriptionId,\n customerId: result.customerId,\n });\n\n await postMessage(\n channelId,\n 'Subscription active',\n buildSubscriptionActiveBlocks({\n result,\n customerName: `${input.firstName} ${input.lastName}`,\n maxioUrl: maxioSubscriptionUrl(result.subscriptionId),\n }),\n );\n\n const payload = {\n txnId: txn.txnId,\n channelId,\n channelName: channelResult.channel?.name ?? null,\n subscription: result,\n };\n session.idempotency[idemKey] = payload;\n session.lastResult = payload;\n sessionStore.put(session);\n\n return res.json({\n status: 'ok',\n ...payload,\n channel: {\n created: Boolean(channelResult.channel) && !channelResult.reused,\n reused: channelResult.reused,\n consultantInvited: channelResult.consultantInvited,\n clientInvited: channelResult.clientInvited,\n clientNotifiedByEmail: channelResult.clientNotifiedByEmail,\n notes: channelResult.notes,\n },\n });\n } catch (err) {\n const message = err instanceof MaxioServiceError ? err.message : `UC1 failed: ${String(err)}`;\n transactionStore.update(txn.txnId, { state: 'failed', lastError: message });\n await postMessage(channelId, 'Booking failed', buildFailureBlocks('Booking', message));\n\n return res.status(200).json({\n status: 'maxio_failed',\n txnId: txn.txnId,\n channelId,\n channelName: channelResult.channel?.name ?? null,\n error: message,\n });\n }\n});\n" }

🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\seed.ts", "content": "import { ApiError, IntervalUnit } from '@maxio-com/advanced-billing-sdk';\nimport { getMaxioClient } from './maxioClient.js';\nimport { PRODUCT_FAMILY, PLANS } from './constants.js';\nimport { formatCents } from './util.js';\n\n/**\n * Idempotent seed for UC1 (plan \u00a71.6, \u00a78 Phase 1 \u2014 products subset). Ensures the\n * MeterMate product family and the flat recurring `basic` ($99/mo) and `pro`\n * ($299/mo) products exist on the configured Maxio test site, each with an\n * explicit price point. Re-running is safe: existing items are detected and\n * skipped. Metered/event components for later use cases are seeded separately.\n *\n * Run with: npm run seed -w server\n */\nasync function ensureProductFamily(): Promise<string> {\n const client = getMaxioClient();\n const { result } = await client.productFamiliesController.listProductFamilies({});\n const existing = result.find((r) => r.productFamily?.handle === PRODUCT_FAMILY.handle);\n if (existing?.productFamily?.id != null) {\n console.log(`\u2022 Product family '${PRODUCT_FAMILY.handle}' exists (id ${existing.productFamily.id}).`);\n return String(existing.productFamily.id);\n }\n\n const created = await client.productFamiliesController.createProductFamily({\n productFamily: {\n name: PRODUCT_FAMILY.name,\n description: 'MeterMate consulting plans and usage.',\n },\n });\n const id = created.result.productFamily?.id;\n if (id == null) throw new Error('Failed to create product family: no id returned.');\n console.log(`\u2713 Created product family '${PRODUCT_FAMILY.handle}' (id ${id}).`);\n return String(id);\n}\n\nasync function ensureProduct(familyId: string, plan: (typeof PLANS)[number]): Promise<void> {\n const client = getMaxioClient();\n try {\n const { result } = await client.productsController.readProductByHandle(plan.handle);\n if (result.product?.id != null) {\n console.log(`\u2022 Product '${plan.handle}' exists (id ${result.product.id}).`);\n return;\n }\n } catch (err) {\n if (!(err instanceof ApiError) || err.statusCode !== 404) throw err;\n // 404 \u2192 does not exist yet; fall through to create.\n }\n\n const created = await client.productsController.createProduct(familyId, {\n product: {\n name: plan.name,\n handle: plan.handle,\n description: plan.description,\n priceInCents: BigInt(plan.priceInCents),\n interval: plan.interval,\n intervalUnit: IntervalUnit.Month,\n },\n });\n console.log(\n `\u2713 Created product '${plan.handle}' (id ${created.result.product?.id}) at ${formatCents(plan.priceInCents)}/mo.`,\n );\n}\n\nasync function main(): Promise<void> {\n console.log('Seeding MeterMate products on Maxio test site\u2026\\n');\n const familyId = await ensureProductFamily();\n for (const plan of PLANS) {\n await ensureProduct(familyId, plan);\n }\n console.log('\\nSeed complete. Plan handles ready: ' + PLANS.map((p) => p.handle).join(', '));\n}\n\nmain().catch((err: unknown) => {\n if (err instanceof ApiError) {\n console.error(`Seed failed (HTTP ${err.statusCode}):`, err.body || err.result);\n } else {\n console.error('Seed failed:', err instanceof Error ? err.message : err);\n }\n process.exitCode = 1;\n});\n" }

Please manually verify via Postman.** **Step 1 — one-time seed (creates `basic`/`pro` on your Maxio test site).** Idempotent; safe to re-run: ``` npm run seed -w server ``` Expect lines like `✓ Created product 'basic' (id …) at $99.00/mo.` and `'pro' … $299.00/mo`. **Step 2 — start the backend:** ``` npm run dev -w server ``` **Step 3 — Postman request:** - Method/URL: `POST http://localhost:4000/api/book` - Header: `Content-Type: application/json` - Body (use **`remittance`** for the first test — `automatic` collection requires a stored payment method in Maxio and will fail without one): ```json { "sessionId": "demo-1", "firstName": "Jane", "lastName": "Doe", "email": "jane.doe@example.com", "consultantId": "c1", "productHandle": "basic", "collectionMethod": "remittance" } ``` **Correct response (HTTP 200):** ```json { "status": "ok", "txnId": "<uuid>", "channelId": "<C... or null>", "channelName": "txn-avery-stone-jane-doe-1", "subscription": { "subscriptionId": 12345, "customerId": 678, "state": "active", "productHandle": "basic", "productName": "Basic Plan", "mrrInCents": 9900, "currency": "USD", "nextAssessmentAt": "…", "currentPeriodEndsAt": "…", "couponCode": null }, "channel": { "created": true, "reused": false, "consultantInvited": …, "clientInvited": …, "clientNotifiedByEmail": …, "notes": [ … ] } } ``` **Also worth verifying:** - **Slack:** a private channel `#txn-avery-stone-jane-doe-1` is created with the bot, with a `:wave: Transaction started` → `:hourglass_flowing_sand: Booking started` → `:tada: Subscription active` (with a *View in Maxio* button) message sequence. If `CONSULTANT_C1_EMAIL` is a workspace member they're invited; the external client falls to email-only (see `channel.notes`). *(Channel creation needs the bot to have `groups:write`/`users:read.email`/`chat:write` scopes — if a scope is missing, billing still succeeds and `notes` will say so.)* - **Idempotency (AC-07):** re-send the identical body with the same `sessionId` → response includes `"idempotent": true`, no duplicate subscription. - **Failure block:** send `"productHandle": "does-not-exist"` → `200 {status:"maxio_failed", error:"…"}` and a `:warning: Booking failed` message in the channel. A stable id is generated once and persisted\n * in localStorage so multi-step flows (and idempotent re-submits) reuse the same\n * server-side session (plan \u00a74.3).\n */\nconst STORAGE_KEY = 'metermate.sessionId';\n\nfunction randomId(): string {\n if (typeof crypto !== 'undefined' && 'randomUUID' in crypto) {\n return crypto.randomUUID();\n }\n return `s-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2)}`;\n}\n\nexport function getSessionId(): string {\n let id = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);\n if (!id) {\n id = randomId();\n localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, id);\n }\n return id;\n}\n\n/** Start a fresh session (used after expiry or on an explicit reset). */\nexport function resetSessionId(): string {\n const id = randomId();\n localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, id);\n return id;\n}\n" }

[];\n}\n\nexport async function book(req: BookRequest): Promise<BookResponse> {\n return postJson<BookResponse>('/api/book', { sessionId: getSessionId(), ...req });\n}\n" }

🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\services\\catalog.ts", "content": "import { getProductFamiliesController, getComponentsController } from '../maxioClient.js';\nimport { PRODUCT_FAMILY } from '../constants.js';\nimport type { ComponentInfo } from '../types.js';\n\n/**\n * Live catalog cache (plan risk mitigation \u00a711): resolves the MeterMate product\n * family id and the `handle \u2192 component` map once, then serves from memory so\n * usage recording can dispatch on the cached component kind without a lookup per\n * request. Loaded lazily on first use; `refresh()` clears it. Any Maxio error\n * during load propagates to the caller (caught and normalized by maxioService).\n */\nlet familyId: number | null = null;\nlet components: Map<string, ComponentInfo> | null = null;\nlet loading: Promise<void> | null = null;\n\nasync function resolveFamilyId(): Promise<number> {\n if (familyId != null) return familyId;\n const { result } = await getProductFamiliesController().listProductFamilies({});\n const match = result.find((r) => r.productFamily?.handle === PRODUCT_FAMILY.handle);\n if (match?.productFamily?.id == null) {\n throw new Error(\n `Product family '${PRODUCT_FAMILY.handle}' not found on the Maxio site. String(c.kind) : 'unknown',\n });\n }\n }\n components = map;\n}\n\nasync function ensureLoaded(): Promise<void> {\n if (components) return;\n if (!loading) {\n loading = loadComponents().finally(() => {\n loading = null;\n });\n }\n await loading;\n}\n\n/** Resolve a component by handle from the live catalog, or null if absent. */\nexport async function getComponent(handle: string): Promise<ComponentInfo | null> {\n await ensureLoaded();\n return components?.get(handle) ?? null;\n}\n\n/** Clear the cache so the next lookup reloads from Maxio (e.g. after seeding). */\nexport function refreshCatalog(): void {\n familyId = null;\n components = null;\n}\n" }

Important realization: the most likely reason `listComponentsForProductFamily` missed the component (pagination or family-scoping on a busy test site) would **also** break the runtime catalog resolution in `catalog.ts`, which uses the same list call. Let me make the catalog robust the same way — resolve each handle via `findComponent` (site-wide, no pagination risk):
🤖 Claude
🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\services\\catalog.ts", "content": "import { ApiError } from '@maxio-com/advanced-billing-sdk';\nimport { getComponentsController } from '../maxioClient.js';\nimport type { ComponentInfo } from '../types.js';\n\n/**\n * Live catalog cache (plan risk mitigation \u00a711). Resolves components by handle\n * via `findComponent` \u2014 which is site-wide and not subject to product-family\n * pagination \u2014 and memoizes the result (including \"not found\") so usage\n * recording can dispatch on the cached component kind without a lookup per\n * request. `refreshCatalog()` clears the cache (e.g. after seeding). Maxio errors\n * other than 404 propagate to the caller (normalized by maxioService).\n */\nconst cache = new Map<string, ComponentInfo | null>();\n\n/** Resolve a component by handle from the live catalog, or null if absent. */\nexport async function getComponent(handle: string): Promise<ComponentInfo | null> {\n if (cache.has(handle)) return cache.get(handle) ?? null;\n\n try {\n const { result } = await getComponentsController().findComponent(handle);\n const c = result.component;\n if (c?.id == null || !c.handle) {\n cache.set(handle, null);\n return null;\n }\n const info: ComponentInfo = {\n id: c.id,\n handle: c.handle,\n name: c.name ?? c.handle,\n kind: c.kind ? String(c.kind) : 'unknown',\n };\n cache.set(handle, info);\n return info;\n } catch (err) {\n if (err instanceof ApiError && err.statusCode === 404) {\n cache.set(handle, null);\n return null;\n }\n throw err;\n }\n}\n\n/** Clear the cache so the next lookup reloads from Maxio (e.g. after seeding). */\nexport function refreshCatalog(): void {\n cache.clear();\n}\n" }

🤖 Claude
Now the full picture is clear, and it overturns my fix. Every new `basic` subscription reliably carries the **product's** metered components — including `metermate-consulting-minutes` (3033453) and `metermate-api-calls` (3033524) — but **never** my separately-seeded `consulting-minutes` (3032114). Critically, the signup `components` array is **ignored for metered components** — the product dictates them. Also notable: `metermate-api-calls` is a **metered** component here, not event-based. So the robust, architecturally-correct fix is: **record usage against the component that's actually on the subscription**, resolved at runtime via `listSubscriptionComponents` (guarantees no 404), and align the app's component handles to the product's real ones. Fixed and verified live end-to-end. Every path works now: | Step | Result | |---|---| | Record `metermate-consulting-minutes` qty 30 | `ok`, periodTotal **30** | | Record again qty 15 | `ok`, periodTotal **45** (running total read back from Maxio) | | Record `metermate-api-calls` qty 100 | `ok`, periodTotal **100** | | Unknown handle `consulting-minutes` | clear error listing the subscription's available components | ## Root cause Usage can only be recorded against a component that is a **line item on the subscription**. In Maxio that means a component the **product** carries — and I confirmed two things empirically against your site: 1. Family components are **not** auto-attached to subscriptions, and the signup `components` array is **ignored for metered components** (the product dictates them). So my first fix — attaching the component at signup — silently did nothing. 2. My seeded `consulting-minutes` (3032114) was a standalone family component never attached to the `basic`/`pro` products, so `createUsage(sub, 3032114)` → 404. The components that *are* on every subscription are the product's: `metermate-consulting-minutes` (3033453) and `metermate-api-calls` (3033524) — both metered, and both accept usage (verified with a direct `createUsage`). (I diagnosed this with a throwaway script against subscription 92665720 and fresh test subscriptions, then deleted it. A few small test-usage records now exist on those test subscriptions — expected test data.) ## The fix (correct, robust approach) - **`maxioService.recordUsage` now resolves the component from the subscription's own line items** (`listSubscriptionComponents`) and records against that `componentId`. This guarantees we only ever target a component on the subscription — no more 404 — and still dispatches on the component's `kind` (metered → `createUsage`; event-based → `recordEvent`). If the requested handle isn't on the subscription, it returns an actionable error listing the available handles. - **`constants.COMPONENTS`** now lists the products' real usage handles: `metermate-consulting-minutes` and `metermate-api-calls` (both metered on your site). - **Removed the ineffective signup-attach** (`buildSignupComponents`) and the **unused site-wide catalog** (`catalog.ts` deleted). - **Seed** now *verifies* the usage components exist via `findComponent` (warns if missing) instead of creating unattached duplicates. > Note: this depends on those two usage components being attached to the `basic`/`pro` products in Maxio (they are, on your site). On a fresh site they'd need to be added to the products in the Maxio UI — the seed now warns if they're absent. Verified by me: `tsc` typecheck + build clean; live flow book → record (×3) → running totals correct → graceful error on unknown handle. **Updated Postman detail:** use `"componentHandle": "metermate-consulting-minutes"` (or `"metermate-api-calls"`) — `GET /api/components` returns the valid handles. Everything else from the prior UC2 message stands. Confirm with **"Okay, backend verified, proceed to the UI"** when ready for the UC2 UI.

🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\routes\\planChange.ts", "content": "import { Router, type Request, type Response } from 'express';\nimport { planChangePreviewSchema, planChangeSchema } from '../schemas/planChange.js';\nimport { sessionStore } from '../stores/sessionStore.js';\nimport { resolveTxn, getTxnChannel } from './txnResolve.js';\nimport { previewPlanChange, applyPlanChange, MaxioServiceError } from '../services/maxioService.js';\nimport { maxioSubscriptionUrl } from '../maxioClient.js';\nimport {\n postMessage,\n buildPlanPreviewBlocks,\n buildPlanChangedBlocks,\n buildFailureBlocks,\n} from '../services/slackService.js';\nimport type { TransactionRecord } from '../types.js';\n\nexport const planChangeRouter = Router();\n\n/** Resolve + guard the transaction; returns the record or sends an error response. */\nfunction resolveOrRespond(\n input: { txnRef?: string; consultantId?: string; email?: string },\n res: Response,\n): TransactionRecord | null {\n const txn = resolveTxn(input);\n if (!txn) {\n res.status(409).json({\n status: 'session_expired',\n message: 'No matching transaction found. Create a subscription (UC1) first, then retry.',\n });\n return null;\n }\n if (txn.subscriptionId == null) {\n res.status(400).json({\n status: 'invalid',\n errors: [{ path: 'txnRef', message: 'transaction has no active subscription' }],\n });\n return null;\n }\n return txn;\n}\n\n/**\n * UC3a \u2014 preview a plan change. Computes the prorated cost of moving to the\n * target plan and posts the computed delta to the transaction channel. No change\n * is applied.\n */\nplanChangeRouter.post('/plan-change/preview', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n const parsed = planChangePreviewSchema.safeParse(req.body);\n if (!parsed.success) {\n return res.status(400).json({\n status: 'invalid',\n errors: parsed.error.issues.map((i) => ({ path: i.path.join('.'), message: i.message })),\n });\n }\n const input = parsed.data;\n const txn = resolveOrRespond(input, res);\n if (!txn || txn.subscriptionId == null) return;\n\n const session = sessionStore.ensure(input.sessionId);\n session.lastSubmission = input;\n sessionStore.put(session);\n\n const channel = getTxnChannel(txn);\n const channelId = channel?.id ?? null;\n\n try {\n const preview = await previewPlanChange({\n subscriptionId: txn.subscriptionId,\n targetHandle: input.targetHandle,\n });\n\n await postMessage(channelId, 'Plan change preview', buildPlanPreviewBlocks(preview));\n\n const payload = { txnId: txn.txnId, channelId, channelName: channel?.name ?? null, preview };\n session.lastResult = payload;\n sessionStore.put(session);\n return res.json({ status: 'ok', ...payload });\n } catch (err) {\n const message = err instanceof MaxioServiceError ? err.message : `UC3 preview failed: ${String(err)}`;\n await postMessage(channelId, 'Plan change preview failed', buildFailureBlocks('Plan change preview', message));\n return res.status(200).json({\n status: 'maxio_failed',\n txnId: txn.txnId,\n channelId,\n channelName: channel?.name ?? null,\n error: message,\n });\n }\n});\n\n/**\n * UC3b \u2014 apply a plan change. `prorate` migrates now with proration; `at-renewal`\n * schedules a non-prorated change for the next renewal. Posts old\u2192new + timing to\n * the transaction channel.\n */\nplanChangeRouter.post('/plan-change', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n const parsed = planChangeSchema.safeParse(req.body);\n if (!parsed.success) {\n return res.status(400).json({\n status: 'invalid',\n errors: parsed.error.issues.map((i) => ({ path: i.path.join('.'), message: i.message })),\n });\n }\n const input = parsed.data;\n const txn = resolveOrRespond(input, res);\n if (!txn || txn.subscriptionId == null) return;\n\n const session = sessionStore.ensure(input.sessionId);\n session.lastSubmission = input;\n sessionStore.put(session);\n\n const channel = getTxnChannel(txn);\n const channelId = channel?.id ?? null;\n\n try {\n const change = await applyPlanChange({\n subscriptionId: txn.subscriptionId,\n targetHandle: input.targetHandle,\n timing: input.timing,\n });\n\n await postMessage(\n channelId,\n 'Plan changed',\n buildPlanChangedBlocks({\n fromName: change.fromName,\n toName: change.toName,\n timing: change.timing,\n effectiveAt: change.effectiveAt,\n maxioUrl: maxioSubscriptionUrl(txn.subscriptionId),\n }),\n );\n\n const payload = { txnId: txn.txnId, channelId, channelName: channel?.name ?? null, change };\n session.lastResult = payload;\n sessionStore.put(session);\n return res.json({ status: 'ok', ...payload });\n } catch (err) {\n const message = err instanceof MaxioServiceError ? err.message : `UC3 plan-change failed: ${String(err)}`;\n await postMessage(channelId, 'Plan change failed', buildFailureBlocks('Plan change', message));\n return res.status(200).json({\n status: 'maxio_failed',\n txnId: txn.txnId,\n channelId,\n channelName: channel?.name ?? null,\n error: message,\n });\n }\n});\n" }

String(result.subscription.state) : before.state };\n }\n case 'reactivate': {\n const { result } = await status.reactivateSubscription(input.subscriptionId, {});\n return { ...base, newState: result.subscription?.state ? String(result.subscription.state) : before.state };\n }\n case 'cancel': {\n const cancelType: CancelType = input.cancelType ?? 'Cancellation scheduled for end of period.',\n };\n }\n const { result } = await status.cancelSubscription(input.subscriptionId, {\n subscription: cancellation,\n });\n return {\n ...base,\n cancelType,\n newState: result.subscription?.state ? String(result.subscription.state) : 'canceled',\n };\n }\n default: {\n const exhaustive: never = input.action;\n throw new MaxioServiceError(`UC4 lifecycleAction: unknown action '${String(exhaustive)}'`, 400);\n }\n }\n } catch (err) {\n if (err instanceof MaxioServiceError) throw err;\n throw toServiceError(err, 'UC4 lifecycleAction');\n }\n}" }

🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\routes\\lifecycle.ts", "content": "import { Router, type Request, type Response } from 'express';\nimport { lifecycleSchema } from '../schemas/lifecycle.js';\nimport { sessionStore } from '../stores/sessionStore.js';\nimport { resolveTxn, getTxnChannel } from './txnResolve.js';\nimport { lifecycleAction, MaxioServiceError } from '../services/maxioService.js';\nimport {\n postMessage,\n buildLifecycleStartedBlocks,\n buildLifecycleDoneBlocks,\n buildFailureBlocks,\n} from '../services/slackService.js';\n\nexport const lifecycleRouter = Router();\n\n/**\n * UC4 \u2014 Lifecycle Control. One route, four actions (pause/resume/cancel/\n * reactivate). Resolves the existing transaction + channel, posts an in-progress\n * note, dispatches to the matching Maxio status operation, and posts the\n * resulting state transition. Slack failures never block the response (plan \u00a76).\n */\nlifecycleRouter.post('/lifecycle', async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n const parsed = lifecycleSchema.safeParse(req.body);\n if (!parsed.success) {\n return res.status(400).json({\n status: 'invalid',\n errors: parsed.error.issues.map((i) => ({ path: i.path.join('.'), message: i.message })),\n });\n }\n const input = parsed.data;\n\n const txn = resolveTxn(input);\n if (!txn) {\n return res.status(409).json({\n status: 'session_expired',\n message: 'No matching transaction found. Create a subscription (UC1) first, then retry.',\n });\n }\n if (txn.subscriptionId == null) {\n return res.status(400).json({\n status: 'invalid',\n errors: [{ path: 'txnRef', message: 'transaction has no active subscription' }],\n });\n }\n\n const session = sessionStore.ensure(input.sessionId);\n session.lastSubmission = input;\n sessionStore.put(session);\n\n const channel = getTxnChannel(txn);\n const channelId = channel?.id ?? null;\n\n await postMessage(channelId, `${input.action} in progress`, buildLifecycleStartedBlocks(input.action));\n\n try {\n const result = await lifecycleAction({\n subscriptionId: txn.subscriptionId,\n action: input.action,\n cancelType: input.cancelType,\n reasonCode: input.reasonCode,\n });\n\n await postMessage(\n channelId,\n `${result.previousState} \u2192 ${result.newState}`,\n buildLifecycleDoneBlocks({\n action: result.action,\n previousState: result.previousState,\n newState: result.newState,\n effectiveAt: result.effectiveAt,\n reasonCode: result.reasonCode,\n note: result.note,\n }),\n );\n\n const payload = { txnId: txn.txnId, channelId, channelName: channel?.name ?? null, lifecycle: result };\n session.lastResult = payload;\n sessionStore.put(session);\n return res.json({ status: 'ok', ...payload });\n } catch (err) {\n const message = err instanceof MaxioServiceError ? err.message : `UC4 failed: ${String(err)}`;\n await postMessage(channelId, 'Lifecycle action failed', buildFailureBlocks('Lifecycle', message));\n return res.status(200).json({\n status: 'maxio_failed',\n txnId: txn.txnId,\n channelId,\n channelName: channel?.name ?? null,\n error: message,\n });\n }\n});\n" }

Resolves the\n * transaction + channel, posts an in-progress note, creates and issues an ad-hoc\n * invoice (optionally emailing it), reads back the hosted public payment URL, and\n * posts the issued invoice with a \"Pay Invoice\" button. Slack failures never\n * block the response (plan \u00a76).\n */\ninvoicesRouter.post('/invoices', adminGuard, async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n const parsed = invoiceSchema.safeParse(req.body);\n if (!parsed.success) {\n return res.status(400).json({\n status: 'invalid',\n errors: parsed.error.issues.map((i) => ({ path: i.path.join('.'), message: i.message })),\n });\n }\n const input = parsed.data;\n\n const txn = resolveTxn(input);\n if (!txn) {\n return res.status(409).json({\n status: 'session_expired',\n message: 'No matching transaction found. Create a subscription (UC1) first, then retry.',\n });\n }\n if (txn.subscriptionId == null) {\n return res.status(400).json({\n status: 'invalid',\n errors: [{ path: 'txnRef', message: 'transaction has no active subscription' }],\n });\n }\n\n const session = sessionStore.ensure(input.sessionId);\n session.lastSubmission = input;\n sessionStore.put(session);\n\n const channel = getTxnChannel(txn);\n const channelId = channel?.id ?? null;\n\n await postMessage(channelId, 'Issuing invoice', buildInvoiceStartedBlocks());\n\n try {\n const invoice = await issueInvoice({\n subscriptionId: txn.subscriptionId,\n clientEmail: txn.clientEmail,\n lineItems: input.lineItems,\n memo: input.memo,\n sendEmail: input.sendEmail,\n });\n\n await postMessage(\n channelId,\n 'Invoice issued',\n buildInvoiceIssuedBlocks({\n number: invoice.number,\n totalAmount: invoice.totalAmount,\n dueAmount: invoice.dueAmount,\n dueDate: invoice.dueDate,\n publicUrl: invoice.publicUrl,\n emailed: invoice.emailed,\n }),\n );\n\n const payload = { txnId: txn.txnId, channelId, channelName: channel?.name ?? null, invoice };\n session.lastResult = payload;\n sessionStore.put(session);\n return res.json({ status: 'ok', ...payload });\n } catch (err) {\n const message = err instanceof MaxioServiceError ? err.message : `UC5 failed: ${String(err)}`;\n await postMessage(channelId, 'Invoice failed', buildFailureBlocks('Invoice', message));\n return res.status(200).json({\n status: 'maxio_failed',\n txnId: txn.txnId,\n channelId,\n channelName: channel?.name ?? null,\n error: message,\n });\n }\n});\n" }

The hardcoded\n * operator credentials are kept in sessionStorage and sent as HTTP Basic auth on\n * admin-guarded routes. The server is the source of truth: a wrong password is\n * rejected with 401 on the first admin action. Clean seam for real auth later.\n */\nconst KEY = 'metermate.adminCreds';\n\ninterface Creds {\n user: string;\n pass: string;\n}\n\nfunction read(): Creds | null {\n try {\n const raw = sessionStorage.getItem(KEY);\n return raw ? (JSON.parse(raw) as Creds) : null;\n } catch {\n return null;\n }\n}\n\nexport function setAdminCreds(user: string, pass: string): void {\n try {\n sessionStorage.setItem(KEY, JSON.stringify({ user, pass }));\n } catch {\n // Ignore storage failures; the header getter falls back to null.\n }\n}\n\nexport function clearAdminCreds(): void {\n try {\n sessionStorage.removeItem(KEY);\n } catch {\n // no-op\n }\n}\n\nexport function hasAdminCreds(): boolean {\n return read() !== null;\n}\n\n/** Returns the `Authorization: Basic \u2026` header value, or null if not logged in. */\nexport function getAdminAuthHeader(): string | null {\n const creds = read();\n if (!creds) return null;\n return `Basic ${btoa(`${creds.user}:${creds.pass}`)}`;\n}\n" }

Credentials are verified against the\n * server before access is granted: we hit the admin-guarded invoices route with\n * a body that intentionally fails validation. Because `adminGuard` runs before\n * body validation, wrong credentials return 401 (rejected here) while correct\n * credentials return 400 (guard passed, no invoice created) \u2014 so any non-401\n * response confirms the credentials are valid. Placeholder for real auth.\n */\nexport function AdminLogin({ onLogin }: { onLogin: () => void }) {\n const [user, setUser] = useState('');\n const [pass, setPass] = useState('');\n const [verifying, setVerifying] = useState(false);\n const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);\n\n async function onSubmit(e: FormEvent) {\n e.preventDefault();\n setVerifying(true);\n setError(null);\n\n const authHeader = `Basic ${btoa(`${user.trim()}:${pass}`)}`;\n try {\n // Empty body fails the route's schema, so a valid guard yields 400 (not a\n // created invoice); an invalid guard yields 401.\n const res = await fetch('/api/invoices', {\n method: 'POST',\n headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', Authorization: authHeader },\n body: JSON.stringify({}),\n });\n\n if (res.status === 401) {\n setError('Invalid credentials. 👤 User
The AdminLogin credential verification is not working correctly in the browser. When wrong credentials are entered, the browser shows its own native "Sign in to access this site" popup dialog instead of the inline "Invalid credentials. Please try again." error message we expect. Even entering correct credentials in that popup keeps looping. The fix should handle the error entirely within the React UI without any browser native dialogs appearing.
🤖 Claude
The native popup isn't something the React code can suppress — it's triggered by the **server's response header**. Our `adminGuard` sends `WWW-Authenticate: Basic realm="..."` on the 401, and browsers automatically show their built-in HTTP-auth dialog whenever a 401 carries a recognized `WWW-Authenticate` scheme. No client-side `fetch` code can stop the browser from acting on that header — so the real fix is to stop sending it on these API 401s (standard practice for XHR/JSON endpoints). The `AdminLogin` component itself is already correct (it handles the 401 inline). Let me confirm the offending line, then remove it:
🤖 Claude

Our `adminGuard` was sending `WWW-Authenticate: Basic realm="MeterMate Admin"`, so the browser intercepted the login `fetch`'s 401 and showed its own popup (which loops because it keeps re-prompting outside React's control). The route still returns `401 {status:"unauthorized", …}` — now the SPA's `fetch` receives it cleanly and `AdminLogin` renders the inline **"Invalid credentials. Please try again."** message. This is the standard approach for XHR/JSON endpoints. `AdminLogin.tsx` was already correct and is unchanged. 🔧 Using tool: Edit Input: { "replace_all": false, "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\services\\maxioService.ts", "old_string": "import { ApiError, CollectionMethod, CreateInvoiceStatus } from '@maxio-com/advanced-billing-sdk';\nimport {\n getSubscriptionsController,\n getSubscriptionComponentsController,\n getSubscriptionProductsController,\n getSubscriptionStatusController,\n getInvoicesController,\n} from '../maxioClient.js';\nimport { centsToNumber } from '../util.js';\nimport { findComponentMeta, findPlan } from '../constants.js';\nimport type {\n CancelType,\n CollectionMethodInput,\n InvoiceLineItemInput,\n InvoiceResult,\n LifecycleAction,\n LifecycleResult,\n PlanChangePreview,\n PlanChangeResult,\n SubscriptionResult,\n UsageResult,\n} from '../types.js';", "new_string": "import {\n ApiError,\n CollectionMethod,\n CreateInvoiceStatus,\n InvoiceStatus,\n} from '@maxio-com/advanced-billing-sdk';\nimport {\n getSubscriptionsController,\n getSubscriptionComponentsController,\n getSubscriptionProductsController,\n getSubscriptionStatusController,\n getInvoicesController,\n getEventsController,\n} from '../maxioClient.js';\nimport { centsToNumber } from '../util.js';\nimport { findComponentMeta, findPlan, findConsultant } from '../constants.js';\nimport { transactionStore } from '../stores/transactionStore.js';\nimport type {\n CancelType,\n CollectionMethodInput,\n DigestResult,\n InvoiceLineItemInput,\n InvoiceResult,\n LifecycleAction,\n LifecycleResult,\n PlanChangePreview,\n PlanChangeResult,\n SubscriptionResult,\n UsageResult,\n} from '../types.js';" }

🔧 Using tool: Edit Input: { "replace_all": false, "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\services\\maxioService.ts", "old_string": " } catch (err) {\n if (err instanceof MaxioServiceError) throw err;\n throw toServiceError(err, 'UC5 issueInvoice');\n }\n}", "new_string": " } catch (err) {\n if (err instanceof MaxioServiceError) throw err;\n throw toServiceError(err, 'UC5 issueInvoice');\n }\n}\n\nconst ACTIVE_STATES = new Set(['active', 'trialing']);\nconst DIGEST_CAVEAT =\n 'Reporting data is for reconciliation, not real-time confirmation; counts may lag live state slightly.';\n\n/**\n * UC6 \u2014 build a per-consultant billing activity digest. The consultant is a\n * MeterMate label, not a Maxio entity, so the consultant's scope is the set of\n * subscriptions MeterMate created for them (from the transaction store). For each\n * subscription it reads live state + MRR, lists open invoices (counting overdue),\n * and counts recent events in the window. Mirrors the Maxio reconciliation\n * caveat (plan \u00a72 UC6).\n */\nexport async function buildDigest(consultantId: string, windowDays: number): Promise<DigestResult> {\n try {\n const consultant = findConsultant(consultantId);\n const txns = transactionStore.findSubscriptionsForConsultant(consultantId);\n\n // Dedupe to unique subscriptions, keeping the earliest creation time.\n const subs = new Map<number, { createdAt: number }>();\n for (const t of txns) {\n const id = t.subscriptionId as number;\n const existing = subs.get(id);\n if (!existing || t.createdAt < existing.createdAt) subs.set(id, { createdAt: t.createdAt });\n }\n\n const windowStartMs = Date.now() - windowDays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;\n const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10); // YYYY-MM-DD\n\n const subscriptions = getSubscriptionsController();\n const invoices = getInvoicesController();\n const events = getEventsController();\n\n let activeCount = 0;\n let mrrInCents = 0;\n let newSignups = 0;\n let churn = 0;\n let overdueInvoices = 0;\n let recentEvents = 0;\n\n for (const [subscriptionId, meta] of subs) {\n if (meta.createdAt >= windowStartMs) newSignups += 1;\n\n const { result: subRes } = await subscriptions.readSubscription(subscriptionId);\n const sub = subRes.subscription;\n const state = sub?.state ? String(sub.state) : 'unknown';\n if (ACTIVE_STATES.has(state)) {\n activeCount += 1;\n mrrInCents +=\n centsToNumber(sub?.productPriceInCents) ?? centsToNumber(sub?.product?.priceInCents) ?? 0;\n }\n if (state === 'canceled') churn += 1;\n\n const { result: invRes } = await invoices.listInvoices({\n subscriptionId,\n status: InvoiceStatus.Open,\n perPage: 100,\n });\n overdueInvoices += invRes.invoices.filter((inv) => inv.dueDate != null && inv.dueDate < today).length;\n\n const { result: evRes } = await events.listSubscriptionEvents({ subscriptionId, perPage: 100 });\n recentEvents += evRes.filter(\n (e) => e.event?.createdAt != null && new Date(e.event.createdAt).getTime() >= windowStartMs,\n ).length;\n }\n\n return {\n consultantId,\n consultantName: consultant?.name ?? consultantId,\n windowDays,\n subscriptionsConsidered: subs.size,\n activeCount,\n mrrInCents,\n newSignups,\n churn,\n overdueInvoices,\n recentEvents,\n caveat: DIGEST_CAVEAT,\n };\n } catch (err) {\n if (err instanceof MaxioServiceError) throw err;\n throw toServiceError(err, 'UC6 buildDigest');\n }\n}" }

🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "E:\\Apimatic-Internship\\MeterMate\\server\\src\\routes\\digest.ts", "content": "import { Router, type Request, type Response } from 'express';\nimport { adminGuard } from '../auth.js';\nimport { config } from '../config.js';\nimport { digestSchema } from '../schemas/digest.js';\nimport { findConsultant } from '../constants.js';\nimport { sessionStore } from '../stores/sessionStore.js';\nimport { buildDigest, MaxioServiceError } from '../services/maxioService.js';\nimport { postMessage, buildDigestBlocks } from '../services/slackService.js';\nimport type { DigestResult } from '../types.js';\n\nexport const digestRouter = Router();\n\n/**\n * Build a consultant's digest and post it to the configured digest channel\n * (plan \u00a77 SLACK_DIGEST_CHANNEL). Returns the digest data and whether it was\n * posted. Shared by the manual route and the (flagged) cron.\n */\nexport async function postDigest(\n consultantId: string,\n windowDays: number,\n): Promise<{ digest: DigestResult; posted: boolean; channelId: string | null }> {\n const digest = await buildDigest(consultantId, windowDays);\n const channelId = config.SLACK_DIGEST_CHANNEL || null;\n let posted = false;\n if (channelId) {\n posted = await postMessage(\n channelId,\n `Billing digest \u2014 ${digest.consultantName}`,\n buildDigestBlocks(digest),\n );\n }\n return { digest, posted, channelId };\n}\n\n/**\n * UC6 \u2014 Billing Activity Digest (admin only). Manual trigger (primary). Builds a\n * per-consultant summary from live Maxio data and posts it to the consultant\n * digest channel.\n */\ndigestRouter.post('/digest', adminGuard, async (req: Request, res: Response) => {\n const parsed = digestSchema.safeParse(req.body);\n if (!parsed.success) {\n return res.status(400).json({\n status: 'invalid',\n errors: parsed.error.issues.map((i) => ({ path: i.path.join('.'), message: i.message })),\n });\n }\n const input = parsed.data;\n\n if (!findConsultant(input.consultantId)) {\n return res.status(400).json({\n status: 'invalid',\n errors: [{ path: 'consultantId', message: `unknown consultant '${input.consultantId}'` }],\n });\n }\n\n const session = sessionStore.ensure(input.sessionId);\n session.lastSubmission = input;\n sessionStore.put(session);\n\n try {\n const { digest, posted, channelId } = await postDigest(input.consultantId, input.windowDays);\n session.lastResult = digest;\n sessionStore.put(session);\n return res.json({ status: 'ok', digest, posted, channelId });\n } catch (err) {\n const message = err instanceof MaxioServiceError ? err.message : `UC6 failed: ${String(err)}`;\n return res.status(200).json({ status: 'maxio_failed', error: message });\n }\n});\n" }

🤖 Claude
Now I have the real root cause. The booking **succeeded** (subscription `92667782`, active, $99 MRR — it just took ~31s due to the transient Slack rate-limit retries). But the digest threw a **Maxio SDK strict-deserialization error** on the events call: `listSubscriptionEvents` failed because one event's `event_specific_data` shape (`{product_id, account_transaction_id}`) isn't in the SDK 9.1.0's expected union — an SDK/API schema mismatch, not our logic. The fix: make the supplementary events read **best-effort** (like `readPeriodTotal`), so a schema hiccup on events never fails the whole digest. The core metrics (active, MRR, signups, churn, overdue) come from subscriptions + invoices, which parse fine.
🤖 Claude
